Syntax

Auxiliary Verbs and Copula

  • This corpus does not contain copulas.

Syntax

Auxiliary Verbs and Copula

  • This corpus uses 5 lemmas as copulas (cop). Examples: y, i, ol, değil, null.

Syntax

Auxiliary Verbs and Copula

  • This corpus does not contain copulas.

Syntax

Auxiliary Verbs and Copula

  • This corpus uses 1 lemmas as copulas (cop). Examples: i.
  • This corpus uses 2 lemmas as auxiliaries (aux). Examples: mi, değil.
  • This corpus uses 7 lemmas as auxiliaries (aux). Examples: ol, değil, dur, i, y, mi, bulun.
  • This corpus uses 2 lemmas as auxiliaries (aux). Examples: mi, değil.
  • This corpus uses 4 lemmas as auxiliaries (aux). Examples: ol, değil, bulun, bil.
  • This corpus uses 4 lemmas as auxiliaries (aux). Examples: i, değil, mi, ol.
  • This corpus uses 2 lemmas as auxiliaries (aux). Examples: mi, değil.
  • This corpus uses 4 lemmas as auxiliaries (aux). Examples: değil, mi, ol, i.
  • This corpus uses 2 lemmas as auxiliaries (aux). Examples: değil, mi.
  • This corpus uses 2 lemmas as auxiliaries (aux). Examples: değil, mi.
  • This corpus uses 4 lemmas as auxiliaries (aux). Examples: ol, değil, dur, i.
